)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@@. ******* *END                            DI

)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@@. ******* *FILE                       - A MODE 4 TYPE DO
)@@G@@FILE SGS IS    *******  @H@@@@. *******                             -   DP

)@@G@@EPEAT LAST' FOLLOWS AN '*IF LAST ....' STATEMENT,  *******  @H@@@@. ****DS
)@@G@@*** THE STATEMENT BEFORE THE '*IF' STATEMENT IS REPEATED UNTIL *******  DT
)@@G@@@H@@@@. ******* THE CONDITION ON THE '*IF' STATEMENT BECOMES TRUE.      DU
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@@. ******* IF A '*REPEAT LAST' FOLLOWS AN SGS IMAGE, THDV
)@@G@@AT SGS IMAGE   *******  @H@@@@. ******* IS REPEATED UNTIL A RESPONSE OF DW
)@@G@@'$END' IS GIVEN.           *******  @H@@@@. *******                     DX
)@@G@@                                       *******  @H@@@@. ******* AN ANSWEDY
)@@G@@R OF '$SKIP' TO ANY SGS QUESTION, WILL SKIP        *******  @H@@@@. ****DZ

)@@G@@ITILIAZE PTRS FOR STRING INPUT@ @@@!          L,U       X2,HDBUFF @ @@@!PY
)@@G@@          L         X3,(1,0)  @E@@@!LOOP1     READ$     IMAGE,INIT      PZ
)@@G@@  . READ NEXT STRING    @D@@@!          L,U       A3,0,A0           . WOQA
)@@G@@RD COUNT    @ @@@!          LXI       A0,A3     @ @@@!          LXM,U   QB
)@@G@@  A0,IMAGE  @A@@@!          A         A0,(0100,0)     @ @@@!          TNQC
)@@G@@Z       BATCH     @F@@@!          PRINT$                      . ECHO INPQD

)@@G@@  .   BY SUBTRACTING TRAILING BLANKS@ @@@!          LMJ       X11,BGET  QH
)@@G@@@ @@@!          TNE,U     A0,' '    @ @@@!          J         LOOP2     QI

)@@G@@@ @@@!          SSL       A1,18     @E@@@!          S,S1      A1,HEAD,*XQN
)@@G@@3       . STORE IN HEAD TABLE @F@@@!          A         A1,A0           QO
)@@G@@  . UPDATE HDBUFF POINTER     @ @@@!          LXI       X2,A1     @F@@@!QP
)@@G@@          INC       NHEAD             . INCREMENT HEAD TABLE COUNT@#@@@!QQ
)@@G@@          NOP     @E@@@!          S         X2,X4             . SAVE HDBQR
)@@G@@UFF PTR     @H@@@!          L,U       X2,ARROW          . SEARCH FOR AN QS
)@@G@@ARROW IN INPUT (->)     @ @@@!          L,U       A1,1,A3   @^@@@!      QT
)@@G@@    L,U       A2,2@A@@@!          LMJ       X11,FINDFIELD   @F@,@!      QU
)@@G@@    J         CONT0A            . NONE FOUND, NORMAL CASE   @F@@@,      QV
)@@G@@    J         CONT2             . NONE FOUND, NORMAL CASE   @G@@@!      QW
)@@G@@    TZ        A0                . IS ARROW IN BEGINNING OF STRING?@B@,@!QX
)@@G@@          J         CONT0             . NO@B@@@,          J         CONTQY
)@@G@@1             . NO@D@@@!          L,T1      A0,HEAD-1,X3      . YES, GETQZ

)@@G@@EAD,X5        . ADD # OF CHARS IN 2ND STRING    @G@@@!          TZ,S4   XH
)@@G@@  HEAD,X5           . IS HEADING A SINGULAR STRING?   @F@@@!          A,XI
)@@G@@U       A0,2              . NO, ADD 2 CHARS FOR '->'  @ @,@!          J XJ
)@@G@@        CONT8     @ @@@,          J         CONT12    @E@,@!CONT7     LXXK
)@@G@@I,S3    X1,HEAD,X5        . GET STARTING CHAR # @E@@@,CONT11    LXI,S3  XL
)@@G@@  X1,HEAD,X5        . GET STARTING CHAR # @D@@@!          AN        X1,(XM
)@@G@@2,0)          . BACKUP TO '->'@D@@@!          L,S4      A0,HEAD,X5      XN
)@@G@@  . GET # OF CHARS@D@@@!          A,U       A0,2              . ADD 2 FOXO
)@@G@@R '->'@G@,@!CONT8     LMJ       X11,BMOVE         . MOVE STRING TO PRINTXP
)@@G@@ BUFFER     @G@@@,CONT12    LMJ       X11,BMOVE         . MOVE STRING TOXQ

)@@G@@    ER        SYMB$             . PRINT HEADING @C@@@!          SP1     XT
)@@G@@  KHEAD             . SET KEY @ @@@!ELOOP5    TLEM      X5,NHEAD  @ @@@!XU
)@@G@@          J         LOOP5     @C@@@!          EXIT$                     XV
)@@G@@  . EXIT    @A@\@!ERR1      PRINT$    MESS4,NMESS4    @#@\@!          EXXW
)@@G@@IT$   @D@@@!ERR2      TE,U      A5,1              . WAS EOF READ? @E@@@!XX
)@@G@@          J         ERR2A             . NO, OTHER I/O ERROR @F@@@!      XY
)@@G@@    TZ        SWAP              . WAS TAPE JUST SWAPPED?    @D@@@!      XZ
)@@G@@    ERR$                        . YES, ERROR    @E@@@!          IOW$    YA
)@@G@@  IOPKT             . READ NEXT RECORD    @ @@@!          L,S1      A0,IYB
)@@G@@MAGE  @G@@@!          TE,U      A0,054            . IS IT AN END-OF-REELYC
)@@G@@ RECORD?    @C@@@!          J         END               . NO, STOP@F@@@!YD

)@@G@@L PROCS NOT DEFINED BY THE *******  @H@@@Q. ******** EXEC 8.  THESE PROCHN

)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@Q. ******** BEING ASSEMBLED.                           HS

)@@G@@                           *******  @H@@@Q. ****************************HU
)@@G@@**********************************************  @D@@@QLIPROC$*  $PROC   HV
)@@G@@  0                 . MASTER PROC   @D@@@QLIPROCS*  $NAME               HW
)@@G@@        . ALTERNATE NAME@H@T@Q          AXR$                        . STHX
)@@G@@ANDARD ASSEMBLER REGISTER NAMES     @H@@@T          $INCLUDE  'MAXR$/'  HY
)@@G@@        . STANDARD ASSEMBLER REGISTER NAMES     @H@@@Q. ****************HZ
)@@G@@**********************************************************  @H@@@Q. ****IA
)@@G@@**** CHECK XQT OPTION $PROC- ISOLATES BIT CORR. TO INPUT LETTER*******  IB
)@@G@@@H@@@Q. ********                                                        IC
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@Q. ******** E.G.  TOPT 'U'    = AND A0,(000000000040)  ID
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@Q. ********       TOPT A2,'U' = AND A2,(000IE
)@@G@@000000040)                 *******  @H@@@Q. ********       AOPT 'U'    =IF
)@@G@@ AND A0,(000000000040)                 *******  @H@@@Q. ********       AIG
)@@G@@OPT A2,'U' = AND A2,(000000000040)                 *******  @H@@@Q. ****IH
)@@G@@****       SOPT 'U'    = TOP A0,(000000000040)                 *******  II
)@@G@@@H@@@Q. ********       SOPT A2,'U' = TOP A2,(000000000040)              IJ
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@Q. ********       GOPT 'U'    = ER OPT$                IK
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@Q. ********                     AND A0,(000IL
)@@G@@000000040)                 *******  @H@@@Q. ****************************IM
)@@G@@**********************************************  @#@@@QP         $PROC   IN
)@@G@@@^@@@QTOPT**    $NAME     0   @^@@@QAOPT**    $NAME     0   @^@@@QGOPT**IO
)@@G@@    $NAME     1   @^@@@QSOPT**    $NAME     2   @A@@@Q          $DO P(0,IP
)@@G@@0)=1 , ER OPT$    @F@@@Q          $DO (P(0,0)<2)**(P(1)=1) , AND A0,(1*/IQ
)@@G@@('Z'-P(1,1)))     @F@@@Q          $DO (P(0,0)=0)**(P(1)>1) , AND P(1,1),IR
)@@G@@(1*/('Z'-P(1,2))) @F@@@Q          $DO (P(0,0)=2)**(P(1)=1) , TOP A0,(1*/IS
)@@G@@('Z'-P(1,1)))     @F@@@Q          $DO (P(0,0)=2)**(P(1)>1) , TOP P(1,1),IT
)@@G@@(1*/('Z'-P(1,2))) @#@@@Q          $END    @[@@@Q.     @H@@@Q. **********IU
)@@G@@****************************************************************  @H@@@QIV
)@@G@@. ******** FORTRAN CALL $PROC                                        ***IW
)@@G@@****  @H@@@Q. ********                                                  IX
)@@G@@         *******  @H@@@Q. ******** CALL SUBR A,B,C,D  = LMJ X11,SUBR    IY
)@@G@@                     *******  @H@@@Q. ********                      + A IZ
)@@G@@                                 *******  @H@@@Q. ********              JA
)@@G@@        + B                                  *******  @H@@@Q. ********  JB
)@@G@@                    + C                                  *******  @H@@@QJC
)@@G@@. ********                      + D                                  ***JD
)@@G@@****  @H@@@Q. ********                      + 0                         JE
)@@G@@         *******  @H@@@Q. **********************************************JF
)@@G@@****************************  @#@@@QCALL**    $PROC   @A@@@Q          LMJG
)@@G@@J       X11,CALL(1,1)   @A@@@QI         $DO CALL(2) , + CALL(2,I) @^@@@QJH
)@@G@@          +         0   @#@@@Q          $END    @[@@@Q.     @H@@@Q. ****JI
)@@G@@**********************************************************************  JJ
)@@G@@@H@@@Q. ******** INFOR TABLE INTERFACE PROCS - AIDS IN USING RINF$, SELTJK
)@@G@@$  *******  @H@@@Q. ********               AND DUSE$ SUBROUTINES        JL
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@Q. ********                                JM
)@@G@@                           *******  @H@@@Q. ******** R$INF - CALLS 'RINFJN
)@@G@@$' AND INVOKES 'ELT$'                  *******  @H@@@Q. ******** S$ELT -JO
)@@G@@ CALLS 'SELT$' WITH PARAMETER #                    *******  @H@@@Q. ****JP
)@@G@@**** D$USE - CALLS 'DUSE$' WITH FILE$NAME(MAY BE R.J.)         *******  JQ
)@@G@@@H@@@Q. ****************************************************************JR
)@@G@@**********  @H@@@QP         $PROC     1    . A PARAMETER SPECIFIES # OF JS
)@@G@@XQT PARAMETERS EXPECTED,@D@@@QR$INF**   $NAME          .      OTHERWISE JT
)@@G@@3 ASSUMED   @F@@@Q          $LEVEL    0,1,0             . MAKE ELT$ LABEJU
)@@G@@LS GLOBAL   @E@@@Q          ELT$                        . INVOKE 'ELT$' JV
)@@G@@PROC  @F@@@Q          $LEVEL    0,0,0             . RETURN TO NORMAL LEVJW
)@@G@@ELING @B@@@QNN        $EQU      28*(3*(P=1)+P(1,1))   @A@@@Q          L JX
)@@G@@        A0,(NN,INF)     @ @@@Q          LMJ       X11,RINF$ @^@@@Q      JY
)@@G@@    J         ERR @^@@@Q          J         CONT@^@@@QINF       RES     JZ
)@@G@@  NN  @ @@@QERR       ER        PRINT$    @ @@@Q          ER        EXITKA
)@@G@@$     @]@@@QCONT      . @#@@@Q          $END    @^@@@QP         $PROC   KB
)@@G@@  1   @#@@@QS$ELT**   $NAME   @A@@@Q          $DO P(1)>0 , L,U A0,P(1,1)KC
)@@G@@@^@@@Q          LMJ X11,SELT$ @#@@@Q          $END    @^@@@QP         $PKD
)@@G@@ROC     1   @#@@@QD$USE**   $NAME   @C@@@Q          $DO P(1)>0 , DL A0,(KE
)@@G@@$CFS(P(1,1)DL))   @ @@@Q          LMJ       X11,DUSE$ @#@@@Q          $EKF
)@@G@@ND    @[@@@Q.     @H@@@Q. **********************************************KG
)@@G@@****************************  @H@@@Q. ******** SOURCE OUTPUT PROCS - AIDKH
)@@G@@S IN USING SSOR, SOR, AND ESOR   *******  @H@@@Q. ********              KI
)@@G@@         SUBROUTINES                         *******  @H@@@Q. ********  KJ
)@@G@@                                                         *******  @H@@@QKK
)@@G@@. ******** S$SOR - SETS UP 'PARTBL', ASSIGNS FILE AND CALLS 'SSOR'   ***KL
)@@G@@****  @H@@@Q. ********         P(1,1) =   FILE $NAME(MAY BE R.J.)       KM
)@@G@@         *******  @H@@@Q. ********         P(1,2) = ELEMENT $NAME(MAY BEKN
)@@G@@ R.J.)               *******  @H@@@Q. ********         P(1,3) = VERSION KO
)@@G@@$NAME(MAY BE R.J.)               *******  @H@@@Q. ********         P(0,1KP
)@@G@@) = 1, IF NOT FIRST TIME CALLED              *******  @H@@@Q. ******** SKQ
)@@G@@$OR  - CALLS 'SOR'                                       *******  @H@@@QKR
)@@G@@. ********         P(1,1) = (NWDS,ADDR)                              ***KS
)@@G@@****  @H@@@Q. ********         P(1,1),P(1,2) = ADDR,NWDS                KT
)@@G@@         *******  @H@@@Q. ******** E$SOR - CALLS 'ESOR'                 KU
)@@G@@                     *******  @H@@@Q. **********************************KV
)@@G@@****************************************  @^@@@QP         $PROC     1   KW
)@@G@@@#@@@QS$SOR**   $NAME   @A@@@Q          $DO P(0,1)=0 , GO CONT1   @B@@@QKX
)@@G@@          DL        A0,($CFS(P(1,1)DL))   @A@@@Q          DS        A0,PKY
)@@G@@ARTBL+27    @B@@@Q          DL        A0,($CFS(P(1,2)DL))   @A@@@Q      KZ
)@@G@@    DS        A0,PARTBL+29    @C@@@Q          $DO P(1)>2 , DL A0,($CFS(PLA
)@@G@@(1,3)DL))   @B@@@Q          $DO P(1)>2 , DS A0,PARTBL+33    @#@@@QCONT1 LB

)@@G@@@A@@@@OPT4      EQU       OPT2++OPT3--1   @G@@@@          DO        OPT4PF
)@@G@@ , MI DIU(1,1),+(OPT$$ F(0)--DIU(1,2)*/-72)     @F@@@@          DO      PG
)@@G@@  OPT4 , DO 36-N(1)<0 , SSA DIU(1,1),N(1)-36    @F@@@@          DO      PH
)@@G@@  OPT4 , DO 36-N(1)>0 , LDSC DIU(1,1),36-N(1)   @#@@@@          END     PI
)@@G@@@[@@@@ .    ___ $END    @[@@@@  .   @^@@@@SNZ2*     PROC      1,2 @^@@@@PJ
)@@G@@W         FORM      36  @E@@@@B(0)      EQU       +(I$ +(EQUF$ SNZ2(1),1PK
)@@G@@,0),SNZ2(0,1))    @F@@@@*[S@@@*SDFF*@^@)@YIDBUFF    'PACKSUB 1R2' @^@@@)PL
)@@G@@IDBUFF    'PACKSUB 1R3' @H@@@X. ****************************************PM
)@@G@@**********************************  @H@@@X. *******                     PN
)@@G@@                                       *******  @H@@@X. *******        PPO
)@@G@@ROGRAM FILE PACK SUBROUTINE                        *******  @H@@@X. ****PP
)@@G@@***                                                            *******  PQ
)@@G@@@H@Y@X. ******* WRITTEN BY LOU INFELD, 02/13/78                         PR
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@Y. ******* WRITTEN BY LOU INFELD, 02/13/78  (1R1)      PS
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@Y. ******* UPDATED BY LOU INFELD, 03/02/78 PT
)@@G@@ (1R2)                     *******  @H@@@). ******* UPDATED BY LOU INFELPU
)@@G@@D, 03/13/78  (1R3)                     *******  @H@@@X. *******         PV
)@@G@@                                                   *******  @H@@@X. ****PW
)@@G@@*** THIS SUBROUTINE WILL SEARCH THROUGH A PROGRAM FILE TO      *******  PX
)@@G@@@H@Y@X. ******* DETERMINE STATISTICS ABOUT THE DELETETED ELEMENTS.      PY
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@Y. ******* DETERMINE STATISTICS ABOUT THE DELETED ELEMEPZ
)@@G@@NTS.           *******  @H@@@X. ******* THIS WILL ALLOW THE CALLING PROGQA
)@@G@@RAM TO DETERMINE WHETHER   *******  @H@@@X. ******* THE FILE NEEDS PACKIQB
)@@G@@NG ACCORDING TO ITS OWN CRITERIA.      *******  @H@@@Y. ******* IF THE EQC
)@@G@@LEMENT TABLE OF FILE IS GREATER THAN 1000 WORDS,   *******  @H@@@Y. ****QD
)@@G@@*** A LARGER BUFFER IS OBTAINED BY 'MCORE$'.                   *******  QE
)@@G@@@H@@@X. *******                                                         QF
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@X. *******         INPUT: A0,A1 - FILENAME (L.J.S.F)   QG
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@X. *******         OUTPUT: A0 - # OF DELETEQH
)@@G@@D ELEMENTS                 *******  @H@Y@X. *******                 A1 -QI
)@@G@@ # OF DELETED TRACKS                   *******  @H@@@Y. *******         QJ
)@@G@@        A1 - # OF DELETED SECTORS                  *******  @H@@@X. ****QK
)@@G@@***                 A2 - TOTAL # OF ELEMENTS                   *******  QL
)@@G@@@H@Y@X. *******                 A3 - TOTAL # OF TRACKS                  QM
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@Y. *******                 A3 - TOTAL # OF SECTORS     QN
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@Y. *******                 A4 - % OF FILE DQO
)@@G@@ELETED                     *******  @H@@@X. *******         CALLING SEQUQP
)@@G@@ENCE: LMJ X11,PACKSUB                  *******  @H@@@X. *******         QQ
)@@G@@                  J ERROR                          *******  @H@@@X. ****QR
)@@G@@***                           J OK                             *******  QS
)@@G@@@H@@@X. *******                                                         QT
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@Y. ******* REVISION SUMMARY                            QU
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@Y. ******* ----------------                QV
)@@G@@                           *******  @H@@@Y. *******                     QW
)@@G@@                                       *******  @H@@@Y. ******* 1R1  -- QX
)@@G@@ FIRST RELEASE                                     *******  @H@@@Y. ****QY
)@@G@@*** 1R2  --  USE MCORE$ ONLY IF ELEMENT TABLE > 1000           *******  QZ
)@@G@@@H@@@Y. *******      --  CORRECTION FOR SMALL FILES                     RA
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@). ******* 1R3  --  CORRECT FOR EMPTY FILE             RB
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@Y. *******                                 RC
)@@G@@                           *******  @H@@@X. ****************************RD
)@@G@@**********************************************  @^@@@X$(1),PACKSUB*     RE
)@@G@@  AXR$@]@Z@Y SLJ TON$   @E@@@Y          S         X10,SAVE          . SARF
)@@G@@VE REGISTERS USED @ @@@Y          S         X5,SAVE+1 @ @@@Y          S RG
)@@G@@        A5,SAVE+2 @ @@@Y          S         X6,SAVE+3 @D@@@X          S RH
)@@G@@        X11,X10           . SAVE RETURN   @E@@@X          DS        A0,FRI
)@@G@@CT            . STORE FILE-NAME     @ @@@X          L,U       A0,FCT    RJ
)@@G@@@ @@@X          LXI,U     X11,PIRCB$@F@@@X          LIJ       X11,BRFTI$RK
)@@G@@        . READ FILE TABLE INDEX     @F@Y@X          TNE,U     A0,2      RL
)@@G@@        . IS FILE PROGRAM FILE?     @E@Y@X          J         0,X10     RM
)@@G@@        . NO, TAKE ERROR EXIT @H@@@Y          J         ERR             RN
)@@G@@  . FILE NOT PROGRAM FILE OR I/O ERROR    @G@@@Y          L,H1      A0,FRO
)@@G@@CT+10         . # OF WORDS IN ELEMENT TABLE     @D@@@)          JZ      RP
)@@G@@  A0,EMPTY          . FILE EMPTY    @E@@@Y          TLE,U     A0,196    RQ
)@@G@@        . MUST BE 196 MINIMUM @ @@@Y          L,U       A0,196    @C@@@YRR
)@@G@@          S         A0,NETBL          . SAVE    @G@@@Y          L,U     RS
)@@G@@  X6,ETBL           . SET X6 TO START OF ELEMENT TABLE@ @@@Y          TGRT
)@@G@@,U      A0,1000   @A@@@Y          L,U       X6,LASTD$+1     @F@@@Y      RU
)@@G@@    A,U       A0,0,X6           . CALC LAST ADDRESS IN TABLE@C@@@Y      RV
)@@G@@    S         A0,LWORD          . SAVE    @F@@@Y          ANU,S3    A0,FRW
)@@G@@CT+11         . CALC ADDRESS OF LAST ENTRY@C@@@Y          S         A1,LRX
)@@G@@ENTRY         . SAVE    @I@@@Y          TG,U      A0,LASTD$         . IFRY
)@@G@@ LAST ADDRESS IN TABLE OUTSIDE OF PROG    @H@@@Y          MCORE$        RZ
)@@G@@              . GET A BUFFER TO HOLD ELEMENT TABLE    @ @@@Y          L,SA
)@@G@@U       A0,FCT    @ @@@Y          LXI,U     A1,0,X6   @ @@@Y          LXSB
)@@G@@M       A1,NETBL  @D@Y@X          JN        A0,0,X10          . I/O ERROSC
)@@G@@R     @ @Y@X          L,U       A0,FCT    @A@Y@X          L         A1,(SD
)@@G@@PFT,1792)   @ @@@X          LXI,U     X11,PIRCB$@G@Y@X          LIJ     SE
)@@G@@  BRPFET$           . READ PROGRAM FILE ELEMENT TABLE @G@@@Y          LISF
)@@G@@J       X11,BRPFET$       . READ PROGRAM FILE ELEMENT TABLE @D@Y@X      SG
)@@G@@    JN        A0,0,X10          . I/O ERROR     @D@@@Y          J       SH
)@@G@@  ERR               . I/O ERROR     @E@@@X          DSL       A0,72     SI
)@@G@@        . INITIALIZE COUNTS   @ @@@X          DSL       A2,72     @E@@@YSJ
)@@G@@          LXI,S3    X5,FCT+11         . # OF WORDS/ENTRY    @G@@@Y      SK
)@@G@@    LXM,U     X5,140,X6         . STARTING LOCATION OF ENTRY TABLE@E@Y@XSL
)@@G@@          L         X5,(10,140)       . SEARCH ELEMENT ITEMS@E@Y@XLOOP  SM
)@@G@@    A,H2      A3,PFT+7,X5       . INCR TOTAL TRACKS   @F@Y@X          A,SN
)@@G@@U       A1,1              . INCR TOTAL # OF ELEMENTS  @F@Y@X          TNSO
)@@G@@        PFT+3,X5          . IS THIS ENTRY DELETED?    @[@@@Y.     @ @@@YSP
)@@G@@.         SEARCH ELEMENT ITEMS@[@@@Y.     @E@@@YLOOP      L,S3      A4,3SQ
)@@G@@,X5           . GET ELEMENT TYPE    @F@@@Y          TN        3,X5      SR
)@@G@@        . IS THIS ENTRY DELETED?    @B@@@X          J         ELOOP     SS
)@@G@@        . NO@F@Y@X          A,H2      A2,PFT+7,X5       . INCR TOTAL DELST
)@@G@@ETED TRACKS @F@@@Y          A,H2      A1,7,X5           . INCR TOTAL DELSU
)@@G@@ETED SECTORS@H@@@Y          TNE,U     A4,5              . IF ELEMENT RELSV
)@@G@@, ADD PREAMBLE SECTORS  @ @@@Y          A,H1      A1,7,X5   @F@@@X      SW
)@@G@@    A,U       A0,1              . INCR # OF DELETED ELEMENTS@D@Y@XELOOP SX
)@@G@@    TLEM,H2   X5,PFT+139        . FINISHED?     @B@Y@X          J       SY
)@@G@@  LOOP              .NO @E@@@YELOOP     A,H2      A3,7,X5           . INSZ
)@@G@@CR TOTAL SECTORS  @H@@@Y          TNE,U     A4,5              . IF ELEMETA
)@@G@@NT REL, ADD PREAMBLE SECTORS  @ @@@Y          A,H1      A3,7,X5   @F@@@YTB
)@@G@@          A,U       A2,1              . INCR TOTAL # OF ELEMENTS  @E@@@YTC
)@@G@@          TLEM      X5,LENTRY         . REPEAT FOR EACH ITEM@^@@@Y      TD
)@@G@@    J         LOOP@D@@@Y          S         A0,A4             . SAVE COUTE
)@@G@@NT    @ @@@Y          L         A0,LWORD  @ @@@Y          TG,U      A0,LTF
)@@G@@ASTD$ @F@@@Y          LCORE$                      . RELEASE BUFFER IF NETG
)@@G@@EDED  @D@@@Y          L         A0,A4             . RESTORE COUNT @^@@@YTH
)@@G@@          SZ        A4  @G@@@Y          JZ        A0,CONT           . IFTI
)@@G@@ NO DELETED ELEMENTS, SKIP    @G@@@Y          L         A4,A1           TJ
)@@G@@  . CALCULATE % OF FILE DELETED     @G@@@Y          DSF       A4,A3     TK
)@@G@@        . SECTORS DELETED / TOTAL SECTORS @E@@@Y          L         A4,ATL
)@@G@@5             . X 100 = % DELETED   @ @@@Y          MF,U      A4,100    TM
)@@G@@@E@@@Y          TG        A5,(0500000000000) . ROUND TO NEAREST % @^@@@YTN
)@@G@@          A,U       A4,1@E@Y@X          J         1,X10             . YETO
)@@G@@S, NORMAL RETURN  @G@@@YCONT      A,U       X10,1             . FINISHEDTP
)@@G@@, TAKE NORMAL RETURN    @ @@@YERR       L         X11,X10   @E@@@Y      TQ
)@@G@@    L         X10,SAVE          . RESTORE REGISTERS   @ @@@Y          L TR
)@@G@@        X5,SAVE+1 @ @@@Y          L         A5,SAVE+2 @ @@@Y          L TS
)@@G@@        X6,SAVE+3 @C@@@Y          J         0,X11             . RETURN  TT
)@@G@@@D@@@)EMPTY     DSL       A0,72             . FILE EMPTY    @ @@@)      TU
)@@G@@    DSL       A2,72     @^@@@-          SZ        A4  @^@@@)          J TV
)@@G@@        CONT@[@@@X$(0)  @^@@@XFCT       RES       47  @^@Y@XPFT       RETW
)@@G@@S       1792@^@@@YLWORD     RES       1   @^@@@YLENTRY    RES       1   TX
)@@G@@@^@@@YSAVE      RES       4   @^@@@YNETBL     RES       1   @^@@@YETBL  TY
)@@G@@    RES       1000@#@@@X          END     ___                           TZ

)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@O. *******      -- GET RUN TYPE FROM NEW LOG LOCATION  GQ

)@@G@@RUNID                      *******  @H@@@O. *******      -- DON'T ASSUMEGS
)@@G@@ 'L' OPTION FOR BATCH MODE             *******  @H@@@O. *******      -- GT

)@@G@@***         BATCH OR BRKPTED RUNS                              *******  GV
)@@G@@@H@@@O. *******      -- REMOVE LOGGING OF EXECUTION                     GW

)@@G@@'              *******  @H@@@O. *******      -- REMOVE TYPE 6 P/O'S     GY
)@@G@@                           *******  @H@@@O. ******* 2R2  -- ASSEMBLE WITGZ
)@@G@@H MASM                                 *******  @H@@@O. *******      -- HA
)@@G@@COMPILE WITH READLG 1R4                            *******  @H@@@O. ****HB
)@@G@@*** 2R3  -- COMPILE WITH READLG 1R5                            *******  HC
)@@G@@@H@@@O. *******      -- CONVERT TO MASM FORMAT                          HD
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@O. ******* 2R4  -- CHANGED LONG LISTING TO 1110 FORMAT HE
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@O. *******      -- COMPILED WITH READLG 1R7HF
)@@G@@                           *******  @H@@@O. *******      -- ADD 'A', 'P'HG
)@@G@@ AND 'S' OPTIONS                       *******  @H@@@P. ******* 2R5  -- HH
)@@G@@UPDATE LONG LISTING TO ALLOW 1100/80 FORMATS       *******  @H@@@P. ****HI
)@@G@@***      -- UPDATE TEST MODE                                   *******  HJ
)@@G@@@H@@@O. *******                                                         HK
)@@G@@   *******  @I@O@N. ****************************************************HL
)@@G@@**************************    @H@@@O. **********************************HM
)@@G@@****************************************  @H@@@O. **********************HN
)@@G@@****************************************************  @G@P@OTEST      $EHO
)@@G@@QU      $PAR(0)**(1*/('Z'-'T')) . TEST MODE IF @MASM,T USED @#@O@N      HP
)@@G@@    AXR$    @G@O@N          ELT$                              . INVOKE 'HQ
)@@G@@INFOR' LABELS     @F@O@N          LIPROCS                           . INHR
)@@G@@VOKE 'SS*LI' PROCS@F@P@O          LIPROC$                           . INHS
)@@G@@VOKE 'LI' PROCS   @E@@@P          LIPROC$                     . INVOKE 'HT
)@@G@@LI' PROCS   @]@@@N$(1),RUNS . @H@P@O          R$INF                     HU
)@@G@@        . READ XQT CARD IN INFOR FORMAT   @G@@@P          R$INF         HV
)@@G@@              . READ XQT CARD IN INFOR FORMAT   @^@P@O          ON      HW
)@@G@@  TEST@E@P@O          COND$                       . GET CONDITION WORD  HX
)@@G@@@D@P@O          AND       A0,(0770000)      . ISOLATE T2    @F@P@O      HY
)@@G@@    TNE       A1,(020000)       . IF = 2, TURN ON SNOOPY    @^@P@O      HZ
)@@G@@    SLJ       TON$@#@P@O          OFF     @G@O@N          AN,U      A4,4IA
)@@G@@                    . SET 'LOPT' IF 'L' OPTION  @G@@@P          TEST    IB
)@@G@@                    . INVOKE TEST MODE IF @MASM,T     @G@@@O          ANIC
)@@G@@,U      A4,4              . SET BATCH KEY IF NOT DEMAND     @F@O@N      ID
)@@G@@    S         A4,LOPT                 .   SPECIFIED OR BATCH@ @@@O      IE
)@@G@@    S         A4,BATCH  @^@O@N          ER        OPT$@F@@@O          ANIF
)@@G@@D       A5,(1*/('Z'-'L')) . SET LOPT IF 'L' OPTION    @^@O@N          TOIG
)@@G@@PT      'L' @ @O@N          OR        A0,LOPT   @ @@@O          S       IH
)@@G@@  A6,LOPT   @F@@@O          AND       A5,(1*/('Z'-'A')) . SET AOPT IF 'AII
)@@G@@' OPTION    @ @@@O          S         A6,AOPT   @F@@@O          AND     IJ
)@@G@@  A5,(1*/('Z'-'P')) . SET POPT IF 'P' OPTION    @ @@@O          S       IK
)@@G@@  A6,POPT   @G@@@O          AND       A5,(1*/('Z'-'S')) . SET PRINTCYCLEIL
)@@G@@ FOR READLG IF    @F@@@O          S         A6,PRINTCYCLE     .   'S' OPIM
)@@G@@TION SPECIFIED    @ @O@N          S         A1,LOPT   @F@@@O          ANIN
)@@G@@D       A5,(1*/34)        . IF PRINT FILE BRKPTED,    @D@@@O          ORIO
)@@G@@        A6,BATCH          .  SET BATCH KEY@ @@@O          S         A7,BIP
)@@G@@ATCH  @E@@@P          S         R11,STYPE         . SAVE COMPUTER TYPE  IQ
)@@G@@@F@@@O          LMJ       X11,IDONLY$       . GENERATE SIGN-ON LINE     IR
)@@G@@@E@O@N          E$DIT     EPRINT                  . EDIT HEADING  @G@O@NIS
)@@G@@          E$COPY    12,('RUN DISPLAY ')     .   (THE DATE USED IS DATE  IT
)@@G@@@F@O@N          E$CHAR    '('                     .    OF COLLECTION)   IU
)@@G@@@^@O@N          E$DAY1    DATE@^@O@N          E$CHAR    '-' @^@O@N      IV
)@@G@@    E$TIME    DATE@^@O@N          E$CHAR    ')' @#@O@N          E$DITX  IW
)@@G@@@E@O@N          P$RINT    (PF 2,6,PRINTB)         . PRINT HEADING @E@O@NIX
)@@G@@          P$RINT    (PF 1,0,0)              . SKIP LINE     @D@@@O      IY
)@@G@@    PRINT$    IDBUFF-3,9        . PRINT SIGN-ON @D@@@O          PRINT$  IZ
)@@G@@  0,0,1             . SKIP A LINE   @F@P@N          SZ        NPO       JA
)@@G@@              . CLEAR NO. OF P/O'S  @E@@@P          SZ        NPO       JB
)@@G@@        . CLEAR NO. OF P/O'S  @E@@@O          SZ        A0              JC
)@@G@@  . CALCULATE OPTION KEY@E@@@O          TZ        LOPT              .   JD
)@@G@@ 'L' OPTION = 3   @^@@@O          L,U       A0,3@E@@@O          TZ      JE
)@@G@@  POPT              .    'P' OPTION = 2   @^@@@O          L,U       A0,2JF
)@@G@@@E@@@O          TZ        AOPT              .    'A' OPTION = 1   @^@@@OJG
)@@G@@          L,U       A0,1@E@@@O          S         A0,KOPT           .   JH
)@@G@@  NO OPTIONS = 0  @I@@@O          L         A0,ACW,A0         . GET CORRJI
)@@G@@ESPONDING READLG ENTRY TYPE ACW     @F@@@O          S         A0,READLGTJJ
)@@G@@        . STORE IN READLG PACKET    @H@O@N          R$INF               JK
)@@G@@              . READ XQT CARD IN INFOR FORMAT   @E@P@N          S$ELT   JL
)@@G@@  1                       . GET RUN-ID    @D@@@P          S$ELT     1   JM
)@@G@@              . GET RUN-ID    @G@O@N          J         RUNE5           JN
)@@G@@        . NO-FIND, ASSUME 'ALL'     @G@P@O          J         RUN0      JO
)@@G@@              . NO-FIND, ASSUME 'ALL'     @F@@@P          J         RUN0JP
)@@G@@              . NO-FIND, ASSUME 'ALL'     @^@@@N          TZ        FNL JQ
)@@G@@@E@O@N          J         RUNE2                   . FORMAT ERROR  @E@P@OJR
)@@G@@          J         RUNE1                   . FORMAT ERROR  @D@@@P      JS
)@@G@@    J         RUNE1             . FORMAT ERROR  @ @O@N          L       JT
)@@G@@  A0,ENL    @^@O@N          TG,U      A0,7@E@O@N          J         RUNEJU
)@@G@@2                   . FORMAT ERROR  @ @O@N          S         A0,RUNL   JV
)@@G@@@H@O@N          L         A0,ENAME                . STORE RUN-ID FOR POSJW
)@@G@@SIBLE DIAG. @E@@@O          DL        A0,ENAME          . GET 1ST PARAMEJX
)@@G@@TER   @ @O@N          S         A0,MESS4V @E@O@N          S         A0,LJY
)@@G@@OGID                . STORE IN LOG  @ @O@N          S         A0,RUNID  JZ
)@@G@@@D@@@O          L         X1,KOPT           . GET OPTION KEY@G@@@O      KA
)@@G@@    DS        A0,*PAR1,X1       . STORE PARAMETER IN CORR LOC     @E@P@NKB
)@@G@@RUN0      S$ELT     2                       . GET START TIME@D@@@PRUN0  KC
)@@G@@    S$ELT     2                 . GET START TIME@F@P@N          SZ      KD

)@@G@@  ENL               . NO FIND, SET TO 0   @E@P@N          TZ        FNL KF
)@@G@@                    . CHECK FORMAT  @D@@@P          TZ        FNL       KG
)@@G@@        . CHECK FORMAT  @E@O@N          J         RUNE6                 KH
)@@G@@  . FORMAT ERROR  @E@P@O          J         RUNE2                   . FOKI
)@@G@@RMAT ERROR  @D@@@P          J         RUNE2             . FORMAT ERROR  KJ
)@@G@@@ @@@N          L         A0,ENL    @^@@@N          TG,U      A0,6@E@O@NKK
)@@G@@          J         RUNE6                   . FORMAT ERROR  @E@P@O      KL
